# Annexation Events
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file

add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Removing temporary ideas
	id = annex.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.0" }
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		remove_ideas = NoDoubleAnnexItalyEvent
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia
	id = annex.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1" }
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.1.a
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = BEL
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = BEL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = WLL
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = WLL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = FLN
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FLN
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2" }
	title = annexation_SWI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SWI_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				760 = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = SWI }
				}
			}
			760 = { add_core_of = SWI }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 943
				is_french_tag = no
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
					943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					any_allied_country = {
						943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = 943 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_german_aid }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_austrian_assisstance }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			SWI = {
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			owns_state = 760
		}
		add_state_claim = 760
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SWI = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SWI_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3" }
	title = annexation_BUL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BUL_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia }
				841 = {
					is_owned_by = SER
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				841 = {
					is_owned_by = SER
					NOT = { is_core_of = SER }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { remove_state_claim = 841 }
			add_state_core = 841
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia }
				106 = {
					is_owned_by = SER
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			add_state_claim = 106
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				has_completed_focus = SER_integrate_macedonia
				106 = {
					is_owned_by = SER
					NOT = { is_core_of = SER }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { remove_state_claim = 106 }
			add_state_core = 106
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
				owns_state = 731
				731 = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			add_state_claim = 731 #Western Salonica
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
				owns_state = 769
				769 = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			add_state_claim = 769 #Eastern Salonica
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
				owns_state = 184
				184 = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			add_state_claim = 184 #Western Thrace
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROM
					tag = RRM
				}
				owns_state = 77
				77 = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				NOT = {
					state = 48 #Sofia
					state = 211 #Burgas
					state = 212 #Plovdiv
					state = 770 #Pleven
					state = 771 #Varna
					state = 1089 #Khardzhali
					state = 1090 #Vidin
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = BUL
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = BUL
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 77 #Silistria
							state = 772 #Dobrudja
						}
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = ROM
								has_subject = RRM
								is_in_faction_with = ROM
								is_in_faction_with = RRM
								owns_state = 46 #Muntenia
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 184 #Western Thrace
							state = 769 #Eastern Salonica
							state = 731 #Western Salonica
						}
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = GRE
								is_in_faction_with = GRE
								owns_state = 47 #Athens
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 767 #Nis
							state = 106 #Macedonia
							state = 841 #Pirot
						}
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = SER
								is_in_faction_with = SER
								owns_state = 107 #Belgrade
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 341 #Adrianople
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = GRE
								has_subject = TUR
								is_in_faction_with = GRE
								is_in_faction_with = TUR
								owns_state = 47 #Athens
								owns_state = 49 #Ankara
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			BUL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BUL }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		BUL = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
						OR = {
							state = 77 #Silistria
							state = 772 #Dobrudja
							state = 184 #Western Thrace
							state = 769 #Eastern Salonica
							state = 731 #Western Salonica
							state = 767 #Nis
							state = 106 #Macedonia
							state = 841 #Pirot
							state = 341 #Adrianople
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = BUL
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			# Pact members asked to give up land
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = SER }
					is_in_faction_with = SER
				}
				country_event = pact.68
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = { id = pact.110 days = 1 }
					country_event = { id = pact.111 days = 1 }
					country_event = { id = pact.112 days = 1 }
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = pact.110 days = 1 }
				country_event = { id = pact.111 days = 1 }
				country_event = { id = pact.112 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Romanian liberation
	id = annex.6
	title = annexation_ROM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ROM_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.6"
		hidden_effect = {
			ROM = {
				remove_ideas = {
					ROM_purged_bucharest_circle
					ROM_royalist_threat
					ROM_everything_for_the_country_idea
					ROM_echipa_mortii_idea
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_russian_tag = yes
						is_ally_with = RUS
						is_ally_with = SOV
						is_ally_with = UKR
					}
				}
				ROM = {
					remove_state_claim = 791 #Podolia
					remove_state_core = 791
					remove_state_claim = 192 #Odessa
					remove_state_core = 192
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = BUL
						owns_state = 48 #Sofia
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_array = { states_to_keep = 77 } #Silistra
				add_to_temp_array = { states_to_keep = 772 } #Dobrudja
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
				OR = {
					78 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					owns_state = 192
					owns_state = 199
					owns_state = 791
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { region = 144 } #Transylvania
				add_to_temp_array = { states_to_keep = THIS }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ROM }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = RRM }
		release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Take Bessarabia
		name = annex.6.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			OR = {
				owns_state = 192
				owns_state = 199
				owns_state = 791
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 78
		add_state_claim = 80
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ROM }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = RRM }
		release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = ROM_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.8" }
	title = annexation_SER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SER_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SER
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 841 #Pirot
							state = 106 #Macedonia
						}
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = BUL
								is_in_faction_with = BUL
								owns_state = 48 #Sofia
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 731 #Western Macedonia
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								has_subject = GRE
								is_in_faction_with = GRE
								owns_state = 47	#Athens
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SER }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		SER = {
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
						OR = {
							state = 841 #Pirot
							state = 106 #Macedonia
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = SER
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #greek liberation
	id = annex.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.10" }
	title = annexation_GRE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_GRE_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.10.a #Liberate Greece as republic
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GRE
					AND = {
						state = 769
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								769 = { is_core_of = BUL }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 48 }
									BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 184
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								184 = { is_core_of = BUL }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 48 }
									BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 766
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								766 = { is_core_of = ALB }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 44 }
									ALB = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 187
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								187 = { is_core_of = OTT }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 773 }
									OTT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
							AND = {
								187 = { is_core_of = TUR }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 773 }
									TUR = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { tag = BUL }
						OR = {
							state = 989 #Salonica
							state = 1076 #Karaferia
							state = 731 #Western Salonica
							state = 769 #Eastern Salonica
						}
					}
				}
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom
				}
				GRE_restore_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				}
				clr_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				set_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.10.b #Liberate Kingdom of Greece
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = GRE
					AND = {
						state = 769
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								769 = { is_core_of = BUL }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 48 }
									BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 184
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								184 = { is_core_of = BUL }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 48 }
									BUL = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 766
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								766 = { is_core_of = ALB }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 44 }
									ALB = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 187
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								187 = { is_core_of = OTT }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 773 }
									OTT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
							AND = {
								187 = { is_core_of = TUR }
								OR = {
									ROOT = { owns_state = 773 }
									TUR = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { tag = BUL }
						OR = {
							state = 989 #Salonica
							state = 1076 #Karaferia
							state = 731 #Western Salonica
							state = 769 #Eastern Salonica
						}
					}
				}
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GRE_memories_of_king }
				remove_ideas = GRE_memories_of_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom }
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GRE_king_alexandros
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GRE_king_georgios
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.26
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GRE_restore_monarchy
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.27
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum
					}
					ROOT = {
						has_elected_government = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum
					has_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
				}
				set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				clr_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_dictatorship_government = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.27
				}
			}
			else = {

						}
					}

country_event = { #Liberation of Croatia
	id = annex.20
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.20" }
	title = annexation_CRO_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CRO_CONQ_desc
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CRO
					NOT = {
						state = 45 #Vojvodina
						state = 103 #Lika
						state = 109 #Posavina
						state = 794 #Syrmia
						state = 163 #Dalmatia
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = CRO
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					163 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ROOT
					163 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CRO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Austria
		name = annex.20.b
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = AUS
			AUS = { AUS_is_unified = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AUS }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = CRO }
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = AUS }
			transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_cores = yes
		}
		else = { transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes }
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = CRO_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Poland
	id = annex.22
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.22" }
	title = annexation_POL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_POL_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = POL_PLC }
					POL_remove_monarchy = yes
					load_focus_tree = KR_Poland
					unlock_national_focus = POL_the_great_debate
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { POL_has_monarchy = yes }
					POL_remove_monarchy = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_democratic_government = no }
				POL = {
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = [RULING_PARTY_TAG]
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						RULING_PARTY_TAG = "[POL.GetRulingIdeologyId]"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.22.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = POL
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = POL
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		POL = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { tag = GER }
					}
					country_event = poland.231
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate only core
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				NOT = {
					state = 10
					state = 87
					state = 90
					state = 92
					state = 97
					state = 98
					state = 1088
				}
				OR = {
					is_core_of = POL
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = POL
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = annex.22.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = POL
						is_claimed_by = POL
					}
				}
				POL = {
					remove_state_core = PREV
					remove_state_claim = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 10
					state = 87
					state = 98
					state = 97
					state = 92
					state = 90
					state = 1088
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			POL = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = POL }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		POL = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { tag = GER }
					}
					country_event = poland.231
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #french option

			add_state_core = 67

				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = NIC
						}
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			ELS = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			ELS = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = ELS_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #The fate of Central Asia
	id = annex.80
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.80" }
	title = annexation_CA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CA_CONQ_desc
	picture = sik_scenery
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = ALO }
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = TRK }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.RUS_kazakhstan_region
				add_core_of = ALO
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.RUS_turkestan_region
				add_core_of = TRK
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #CAF
		name = annex.80.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ALO }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_CAF
		}
	}

	option = { #Divide major
		name = annex.80.b
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 405 #Bukhara
			owns_state = 586 #Pishpek
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		#Alash
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_russian_tag = no }
			ALO = { set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_KAZ }
		}
		
		#Turkestan
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #divide minors
		name = annex.80.c
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 405 #Bukhara
			owns_state = 584 #Karakum
			owns_state = 585 #Kyzyl Kum
			owns_state = 586 #Pishpek
			owns_state = 732 #Ferghana
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }
		#Kyrgyzstan
		KYR = { add_state_core = 586 } #Pishpek
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KYR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		#Tajikistan
		TAJ = { add_state_core = 732 } #Ferghana
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TAJ }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		#Uzbekistan
		UZB = {
			add_state_core = 405 #Bukhara
			add_state_core = 585 #Kyzyl Kum
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = UZB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		#Alash
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_russian_tag = no }
			ALO = { set_cosmetic_tag = ALO_KAZ }
		}
		
		#Turkestan
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russian ally
		name = annex.80.e
		trigger = {
			any_allied_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ALO }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRK }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.80.f
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = CA_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Arabia

	id = annex.106
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.106" }
	title = annexation_SAU_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SAU_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #release a puppet Arabia
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = IRQ
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		name = annex.106.b

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = JBS
					is_core_of = SAU
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 754
							state = 679
						}
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								tag = EGY
								tag = JOR
								tag = OTT
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 907
						ROOT = {
							NOT = { tag = PER }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28
					region = 239
				}
			}

			IRQ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = IRQ }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = SAU }
			}
			every_state = {	
				limit = { is_core_of = SAU }
				remove_core_of = SAU
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = JBS }
			}
			every_state = {	
				limit = { is_core_of = JBS }
				remove_core_of = JBS
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to ally arabia
		trigger = {
			country_exists = IRQ
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = IRQ
				IRQ = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		name = annex.106.c

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = JBS
					is_core_of = SAU
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 754
							state = 679
						}
						NOT = {
							ROOT = { tag = EGY }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28
					region = 239
				}
			}

			IRQ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = SAU }
			}
			every_state = {	
				limit = { is_core_of = SAU }
				remove_core_of = SAU
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = JBS }
			}
			every_state = {	
				limit = { is_core_of = JBS }
				remove_core_of = JBS
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						country_exists = IRQ
					}
					is_in_faction_with = IRQ
					IRQ = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		occupy_medium_country = yes

		set_country_flag = SAU_CONQ
	}
}

	id = annex.109
	title = annexation_PER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PER_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.109"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = OTT
				}
				add_state_claim = 413
				add_state_claim = 421
				add_state_claim = 417
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = SAU
						tag = JBS
					}
				}
				add_state_claim = 413
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = PER
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = PER
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
					AND = {
						state = 352 #Van
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								owns_state = 291 #Baghdad
								owns_state = 49 #Ankara
							}
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28 #Syria
					region = 129 #Anatolia
					region = 239 #Mesopotamia
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 418 #Golestan
							state = 420 #Mazandaran
							state = 804 #Northern Khorasan
						}
						ROOT = { is_russian_tag = yes }
					}
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_elected_government = no
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_authoritarian_government = no
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #iran and kurdistan

		name = annex.109.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = OTT
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = KUR
				KUR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			KUR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = KUR
					KUR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KUR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = PER
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = PER
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28
					region = 129
					region = 239
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_elected_government = no
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_authoritarian_government = no
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		occupy_medium_country = yes

		set_country_flag = PER_CONQ
	}
}

			}

		}
	}

		}

			factor = 1000
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes

			limit = { is_core_of = CUB }

			}

				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }

			}

country_event = { #The fate of Ceylon

	id = annex.119
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.119" }
	title = annexation_CEY_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CEY_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				tag = INR
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 422
					is_core_of = CEY
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CEY = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEY }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #puppet as an Indian

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				tag = INR
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = CEY
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CEY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEY }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		remove_state_core = 422
	}

	option = { #Integrate

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				tag = INR
			}
		}

		name = annex.119.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}

		occupy_small_country = yes

		add_state_core = 422

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ
	}

	option = { #occupation

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				tag = INR
			}
		}

		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		occupy_medium_country = yes

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ
	}
}

		if = {

					is_owned_by = ROOT

				}
			}
			73 = { add_core_of = CZE } #Transcarpathia
		}
		if = {

			if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = yes }
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Vavro Srobar"
							desc = "POLITICS_VAVRO_SROBAR_DESC"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/SVK/Portrait_SVK_Vavro_Srobar.tga"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = [OVERLORD_IDEOLOGY]
						}
					}
					OVERLORD_IDEOLOGY = "[ROOT.GetRulingIdeologySubtype]"
				}
				set_country_flag = was_puppeted
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to Austria
		name = annex.122.c
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = AUS
			AUS = { AUS_is_unified = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AUS }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = CZE }
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = AUS }
			transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_cores = yes
		}
		else = { transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes }
	}

	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CZE_CONQ
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						country_exists = CAF
						OR = {
							tag = CAF
							is_in_faction_with = CAF
						}
					}
					AND = {
						tag = GBR
						has_country_flag = CAF_dissolved
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1078
						state = 1079
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = VEN }
					remove_claim_by = VEN
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = VEN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Occupy Venezuela
		name = annex.139.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = VEN_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Belarus
	id = annex.147
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.147" }
	title = annexation_WHR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_WHR_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.147.a #Liberate White Ruthenia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = WHR
					state = 94
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = WHR
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			WHR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WHR }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 243
					owns_state = 242
					owns_state = 755
					owns_state = 210
					owns_state = 880
				}
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 219
					has_war_with = RUS
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 243
						state = 242
						state = 755
						state = 210
						state = 880
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				WHR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.147.b #Give to Russia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				RUS = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = WHR_RUS_SPHERE
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WHR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			RUS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.147.c #Liberate White Ruthenia as Germany
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
		set_global_flag = WHR_GER_DOW
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = WHR
					state = 94
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = WHR
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			WHR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WHR }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		WHR = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_political_party = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 60
			}
			clr_country_flag = sigismund_I_HoS
		}
	}

	option = { #Occupy White Ruthenia
		name = annex.147.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = WHR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Slovakia
	id = annex.148
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.148" }
	title = annexation_SVK_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SVK_CONQ_desc
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 73 } #Transcarpathia
				SVK = { add_state_core = 73 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 664 } #Southern Slovakia
				SVK = { add_state_core = 664 }
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.148.a #Liberate Slovakia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SVK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Austria
		name = annex.148.b
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = AUS
			AUS = { AUS_is_unified = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AUS }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = SVK }
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = AUS }
			transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_cores = yes
		}
		else = { transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes }
	}

	option = { #Occupy Slovakia
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SVK_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Transylvania
	id = annex.149
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.149" }
	title = annexation_TRS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_TRS_CONQ_desc
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 875
					OR = {
						owns_state = 109
						NOT = { is_ally_with = 109.owner }
					}
				}
				TRS = { add_state_core = 875 }
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Liberate Transylvania
		name = annex.149.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ally_with = AUS
						AUS = { AUS_is_unified = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						is_ally_with = HUN
						84 = { is_core_of = HUN }
					}
					is_ally_with = ROM
					is_ally_with = RRM
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRS }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Austria
		name = annex.149.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = AUS }
			is_ally_with = AUS
			AUS = {
				OR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = DNF
					has_cosmetic_tag = AUS_united_states
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AUS }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRS }
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = AUS }
			transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_cores = yes
		}
		else = { transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes }
	}

	option = { #Give to Hungary
		name = annex.149.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HUN
			84 = { is_core_of = HUN }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HUN }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRS }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.149.d #Give to Romania
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ally_with = ROM
				is_ally_with = RRM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ally_with = RRM }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RRM }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRS }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_cores = yes
	}

	option = { #Occupy Transylvania
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = TRS_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Albania Liberation
	id = annex.152
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.152" }
	title = annexation_ALB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ALB_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.152.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = AUS
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

	}

	option = { #liberate for austria (wied option)
		name = annex.152.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}

		trigger = {
			tag = AUS
			ALB = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ALB_wieddead
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		ALB = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Wilhelm zu Wied"
				desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_WIED_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Albania_Wilhelm_Wied.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}

			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = "Grafschaft Wied-Neuwied"
				name = "Grafschaft Wied-Neuwied"
			}

			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.4
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}

			set_country_flag = ALB_restoration_of_wied
		}
	}

	option = { #take Northern Epirus
		name = annex.152.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = GRE
			owns_state = 766
		}

		ALB = {
			remove_state_core = 766
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = ALB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Netherlands Liberation
	id = annex.154
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.154" }
	title = annexation_HOL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_HOL_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			HOL = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.154.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = BEL
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
		}

		HOL = {
			add_state_core = 979
			add_state_core = 978
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		country_event = {
			id = hol.4
			days = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			country_event = hol.4
		}
	}

	option = { #Restore to the government in exile
		name = annex.154.f
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = DEI
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 160
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HOL
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			DEI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate but give Limburg and Zeeuws-Vlaanderen to Belgium/Flanders-Wallonia
		name = annex.154.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = BEL
					OR = {
						tag = BEL
						is_in_faction_with = BEL
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = FLN
					OR = {
						tag = FLN
						is_in_faction_with = FLN
					}
				}
				AND = {
					tag = FRA
					owns_state = 6
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = BEL_CONQ
						NOT = {
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				978 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				979 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		978 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}
		979 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				978 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = FRA
							tag = NFA
							tag = BEL
							tag = WLL
							tag = FLN
							AND = {
								is_german_tag = yes
								781 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes } #Western Rhineland
							}
						}
						6 = { is_claimed_by = ROOT } #Flanders
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = BEL
				}
				BEL = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					WLL = {
						owns_state = 6
					}
				}
				WLL = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FLN
				}
				FLN = {
					transfer_state = 978
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				979 = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = BEL
				}
				BEL = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					WLL = {
						owns_state = 6
					}
				}
				WLL = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FLN
				}
				FLN = {
					transfer_state = 979
				}
			}
		}

		country_event = {
			id = hol.4
			days = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate but keep Limbourg
		name = annex.154.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GRU #For the future
			}
		}

		978 = {
			remove_core_of = HOL
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		country_event = {
			id = hol.4
			days = 2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.154.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						tag = BEL
						OR = {
							has_government = national_populist
							has_government = paternal_autocrat
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = HOL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = DEI
			}
			country_event = holex.41
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Denmark Liberation
	id = annex.155
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.155" }
	title = annexation_DEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_DEN_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate as monarchy
		name = annex.155.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98

		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = DEN }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		DEN = {
			clr_country_flag = den_hybrid
			clr_country_flag = den_danish_republic
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			DEN = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						date < 1947.05.20
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Christian X"
						desc = "CHRISTIAN_X_DESC"
						picture = "Portrait_Denmark_Christian_X.tga"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {

				add_state_core = 6
			}
		}

country_event = { #Fate of Southern Wallonia
	id = annex.162
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.162" }
	title = annexation_WLL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_WLL_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet Wallonia
		name = annex.162.a
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 34
			NOT = {
				country_exists = WLL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = BEL
					BEL = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			WLL = {
				add_state_core = 34
				add_state_core = 741
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = WLL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		WLL = {
			clr_country_flag = BEL_SYN_REV
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Revolution_By_Force
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists }
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Peacefull_Transition
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Reform_Into_A_Republic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_The_Government_Has_Failed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_The_Government_Has_Failed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			WLL = {
				complete_national_focus = WLL_Hold_On_To_The_Monarchy
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Belgium
		name = annex.162.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = BEL
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BEL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = SRI
					SRI = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = WLL_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Australasia
	id = annex.171
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.171" }
	title = annexation_AST_CONQ
	desc = annexation_AST_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Puppet Australasia
		name = annex.171.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GBR
						tag = CAN
						is_in_faction_with = ENT
					}
				}
				AST = { AST_become_republic = yes }
			}
			else = {
				NZL = {
					random_unit_leader = {
						limit = { has_id = 2100 } #Thomas Blamey
						set_nationality = AST
					}
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = AST
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 757
							state = 737
							state = 634
							state = 734
							state = 635
						}
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								tag = GEA
								tag = GEX
								tag = GER
								tag = JAP
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Release New Zealand
		name = annex.171.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 284
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GBR
						tag = CAN
						is_in_faction_with = ENT
					}
				}
				NZL = { NZL_become_republic = yes }
			}
		}

		NZL = {
			add_state_core = 284
			add_state_core = 723
		}
		AST = {
			remove_state_core = 284
			remove_state_core = 723
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NZL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = GBR
						tag = CAN
						is_in_faction_with = ENT
					}
				}
				AST = { AST_become_republic = yes }
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = AST
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 757
							state = 737
							state = 634
							state = 734
							state = 635
						}
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								tag = GEA
								tag = GEX
								tag = GER
								tag = JAP
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		AST = {
			set_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = AST_CONQ
	}
}

				has_event_target = northwest_war_ally
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 353
						state = 604
						state = 621
						state = 616
						state = 348
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
					add_state_claim = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Release XSM
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = XSM
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = XSM
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = XSM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		setup_puppet_leader_XSM = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = XSM_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Brazil
	id = annex.181
	title = annexation_BRA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BRA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.181"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = PAR }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 1041 #Iguassu
							state = 1042 #Clevelandia
							state = 1043 #Ponta Pora
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = PAR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ARG }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_core_of = BRA
						region = 203 #Uruguay Basin
					}
					add_claim_by = ARG
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate full brazil
		name = annex.181.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BRA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = national_populist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Imperial
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_AIB
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Vargas
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_new_state
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						has_democratic_government = yes
					}
				}
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Democratic
						keep_completed = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						AND = {
							has_government = social_democrat
							has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
						}
					}
				}
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Anarchist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_f_anarchist_b
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Syndicalist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_syndicalist_alliance
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = totalist }
				BRA = {
					load_focus_tree = {
						tree = Brazil_Focus_Totalist
						keep_completed = yes
					}
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_ato_institucional_1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Balkanise Brazil
		name = annex.181.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = ARG
			}
		}
		setup_brazilian_splinters = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PIR }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAH }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SPO }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AMA }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRP }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GOY }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RJM }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Argentina
	id = annex.182
	title = annexation_ARG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARG_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.182"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = ENT
						tag = GBR
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 299 #Falklands
							state = 720 #South Georgia Islands
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = PAR }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 901 #Chaco Austral
							state = 1074 #Corrientes
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = BOL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_core_of = ARG
						OR = {
							region = 204 #Gran Chaco
							state = 903 #Jujuy
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = CHL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						is_core_of = ARG
						OR = {
							state = 512 #Chubut
							state = 1028 #Tierra del Fuego
							state = 1029 #Santa Cruz
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_democratic_government = no }
				ARG = {
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = [RULING_PARTY_TAG]
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						RULING_PARTY_TAG = "[ARG.GetRulingIdeologyId]"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate full argentina
		name = annex.182.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = BRA
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = ARG
				is_ally_with = FOP
			}
		}
		if = {
            limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
            set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FOP }
        }
        else = {
            set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARG }
        }
        add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ARG }
        add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = FOP }
        release_targeted_tag_from_core_regions = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BRA
				has_government = national_populist
			}
			ARG = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Miguel de Andrea"
					desc = "POLITICS_MIGUEL_DE_ANDREA_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_Argentine_miguel_de_andrea.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = national_populist_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate argentina and patagonia
		name = annex.182.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = BRA
			has_government = national_populist
			owns_state = 512

				name = "Antoine III"

			}

			}
		}

		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Miguel de Andrea"
				desc = "POLITICS_MIGUEL_DE_ANDREA_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Argentine_miguel_de_andrea.tga"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
		}

country_event = { #Annexation of Korea
	id = annex.183
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.183" }
	title = annexation_KOR_CONQ
	desc = annexation_KOR_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Liberate a loyal Republic
		name = annex.183.a

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = QIE
					NOT = { has_country_flag = QIE_coup_failed }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = SQI
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		KOR = {
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = KOR_KING }
					kill_ideology_leader = social_democrat
					kill_ideology_leader = social_liberal
					kill_ideology_leader = market_liberal
					kill_ideology_leader = social_conservative
					kill_ideology_leader = authoritarian_democrat
					kill_ideology_leader = paternal_autocrat
					kill_ideology_leader = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KOR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate the Joseon Kingdom
		name = annex.183.b

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tag = QIE
					NOT = { has_country_flag = QIE_coup_failed }
				}
				AND = {
					tag = SQI
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		KOR = {
			hidden_effect = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Yi Kang"
					picture = "Portrait_KOR_Yi_Kang.tga"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = national_populist_subtype
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KOR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		KOR = { set_cosmetic_tag = KOR_KING }
	}

	option = { #Occupy it
		name = annex.183.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = KOR_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Choosing the new Irish Head of State

	id = annex.184
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.184" }
	title = annex.184.t
	desc = annex.184.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Hugo O'Neill

		name = annex.184.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}

		IRE = {
			country_event = annex.185
		}
	}

	option = { #let them decide

		name = annex.184.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Aodh II arrives!

	id = annex.185
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.185" }
	title = annex.185.t
	desc = annex.185.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {

		name = annex.185.a
		set_country_flag = IRE_o'neill_restoration
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Aodh II O'Neill"
			picture = "Portrait_Ireland_Hugo_O'Neill.tga"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = national_populist_subtype
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Canada
	id = annex.188
	title = annexation_CAN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CAN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.188"
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAN }
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
			CAN = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CAN_republic
				CAN_create_republic = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Canada
		name = annex.188.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRA
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAN }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Canada and Quebec
		name = annex.188.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				tag = ENG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				tag = NFA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = FRA
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAN }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Quebec and annex Canada
		name = annex.188.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #Annex Canada
		name = annex.188.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Angola
	id = annex.190
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.190" }
	title = annexation_ANG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ANG_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.190.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 540
					state = 914
					state = 916
					state = 917
					state = 959
					is_core_of = ANG
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ANG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ANG }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = ANG_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Somalia

	id = annex.192
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.192" }
	title = annexation_SOM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SOM_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #SOM

		name = annex.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SOM
					AND = {
						state = 944 #Harar
						NOT = {
							ROOT = { owns_state = 271 } #Can release Ethiopia
							any_country = {
								is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
								PREV = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						state = 892 #Jubaland
						NOT = {
							ROOT = { owns_state = 970 } #Can release Kenya
							any_country = {
								is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
								PREV = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SOM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SOM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupation

		name = annex.192.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SOM_CONQ

		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Namibia
	id = annex.193
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.193"
	}
	title = annexation_NAM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NAM_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.193.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NAM }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			NAM = { complete_national_focus = NAM_syndicalist_liberation }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			NAM = { complete_national_focus = NAM_stern_state }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			NAM = { complete_national_focus = NAM_democratic_mandate }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = NAM_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Gabon
	id = annex.202
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.202"
	}
	title = annexation_GAB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_GAB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.202.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 297
			}
			GAB = {
				add_state_core = 297
			}
		}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.210" }
	title = annexation_LIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LIB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					"LIB" = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b

			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes

country_event = { #Cyprus Liberation
	id = annex.224
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.224" }
	title = annexation_CYP_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CYP_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.224.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		CYP = {
			add_state_core = 183
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CYP }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to the Turks
		name = annex.224.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				TUR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				is_in_faction_with = OTT
				OTT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = TUR
					TUR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				transfer_state = 183
			}
			else = {
				OTT = {
					transfer_state = 183
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to Greece
		name = annex.224.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GRE
				GRE = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		GRE = {
			transfer_state = 183
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CYP_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Indonesia
	id = annex.225
	title = annexation_INS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_INS_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.225"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = DEI }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = DEI }
					remove_core_of = DEI
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = JAP }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = JAP
						is_indonesia = yes
						NOT = {
							state = 333 #North Borneo
							state = 828 #Sabah
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.225.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
				has_subject = GEA
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INS }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		INS = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_INDIES
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { tag = JAP }
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to HOL
		name = annex.225.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HOL
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to GEA
		name = annex.225.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = yes
			is_ally_with = GEA
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEA }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = INS_CONQ
	}
}

		}

							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}

					country_exists = KUR
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KUR = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KUR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #give to JOR ally
		name = annex.239.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JOR

				is_in_faction_with = JOR
				JOR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				819 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			JOR = {
				add_state_core = 819
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
